### [220] [Static Metrics Are Insufficient: Predicting Java Method Energy Usage with Execution Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06124)
*Muhammad Imran,Vincenzo Stoico,Ivano Malavolta*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在Java方法级别基于静态代码指标和执行时间预测能耗的可行性。实验分析了2,786个Java方法，发现仅靠静态代码指标预测效果极差（R²接近0），而加入执行时间后R²提升至0.46。执行时间、内部方法调用次数和圈复杂度是最重要的预测因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件系统的能耗日益成为环境和经济问题，而早期开发阶段进行能耗评估可以帮助开发者做出更优的设计和重构决策。然而，在没有重复性能分析和直接测量的情况下评估能耗非常困难，这限制了早期能耗推理的实际应用。

Method: 对2,786个Java方法进行性能分析，提取33个静态特征，并测量执行时间和能耗。训练并比较了11种回归模型，评估静态代码指标以及结合执行时间对能耗预测的效果。

Result: 静态代码指标单独预测能耗的性能极差（平均R²接近0）。引入执行时间作为轻量级动态输入后，预测精度显著提升，R²最高可达0.46。执行时间、内部方法调用次数和圈复杂度是最强的能耗预测因子。

Conclusion: 仅依靠静态代码指标无法有效预测Java方法的能耗，必须结合动态信息（如执行时间）才能获得有意义的预测结果。该发现为早期开发阶段的能耗评估方法提供了重要指导。

Abstract: The increasing energy demand of software systems is raising concerns about their environmental impact and associated costs. Reasoning on energy usage early in the development flow has the potential to significantly reduce the overall energy usage of a software system, as it allows developers to make informed design and refactoring decisions before inefficiencies propagate. However, assessing energy usage without repeated profiling and direct measurement is difficult, which limits early reasoning in practice. This study investigates the limits of method-level energy prediction in Java, examining whether static source code metrics complemented with method-level execution time can estimate the energy consumption of Java methods. We profile 2,786 Java methods to extract 33 static features and measure execution time and energy, then train and compare eleven regression models. Our findings show that static source code metrics alone yield poor predictive performance, with average R2 values close to zero. Incorporating execution time as a lightweight dynamic input significantly improves accuracy, raising R2 to as high as 0.46.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Neural decompilation is increasingly studied as a code-generation problem, yet its evaluation methodology remains underdeveloped for modern languages. Our study yields three principal findings grounded in paired task-level statistical tests. First, no fine-tuning configuration produces a statistically significant pass@k improvement. The sole positive case yields +0.71 pp (McNemar p=0.21), while fine-tuning the strongest base (Qwen3-8B) causes a highly significant regression of -5.65 pp (p<0.001). This capacity-dependent trend is consistent across architectures but needs broader scale sweeps. Second, cross-lingual interference from Swift training is highly significant at 4B (-2.66 pp, p<0.001) but statistically indistinguishable from zero at 8B, consistent with the scaling hypothesis. Third, we demonstrate metric divergence: CodeBLEU and compile@k can improve significantly while pass@k moves in the opposite direction. This has implications for any LLM code generation task where fine-tuning targets superficial similarity. Error analysis reveals assembly sequence length is the strongest predictor of task difficulty (p=0.001), with a capability cliff at 200 instructions. We contribute the HumanEval-Dart benchmark, a Dart-adapted CodeBLEU, and empirical evidence that pass@k must be the primary evaluation metric for neural decompilation.

### [223] [A Global Author-Identity Map for the World of Code:62.7M Developer Identities from 106.8M Author Strings over 5.87B Commits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06183)
*Audris Mockus*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Mining software repositories at global scale founders on author identity: the same developer commits under many name/email strings, and the same string is reused by many developers. The map is mega-cluster free, its largest cluster 6,910 ids (one GitHub noreply identity), and it resolves 73.5% of six billion commits into multi-id identities, raising human-id commit coverage to 98.17%. The design problem is clumping, not recall: a naive transitive union over shared-attribute edges welds three million unrelated people into one cluster, an over-merge that recall-only benchmarks price at zero. We report both error families, splitting and clumping, and show the high precision claimed by global-scale union maps can be an artifact of never measuring the conflated region. Against the ALFAA human-rated gold set the map scores recall 0.70 / precision 0.88, where the prior WoC map's apparent 0.95 precision collapses to 0.52 once its 3,006,318-id mega-cluster is counted. A canonical software-author identity is also a cross-corpus join key to scholarly author graphs, where clumping is again the binding constraint. All artifacts ship with the WoC V2604 release and a self-contained replication package.

### [224] [What Resolve Rate Hides: Trajectory Structure Diagnostics for Coding Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06184)
*Rui Shu,Chun Yong Chong,Xin Zhou,Yun Peng,Zihan Wu,Xu Han,Zeyang Zhuang,Guowen Yuan,Yuan Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出TraceProbe框架，将编码智能体的轨迹标准化为九类动作，通过规则模块揭示隐藏信息。分析2500条轨迹后发现：函数级行为比文件级更能区分成败；反模式主要反映整体难度；已解决问题的轨迹在效率上仍有差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前编码智能体仅用通过率评估，无法揭示为何失败或为何成功却浪费资源，过程信息完全丢失。

Method: 将原始轨迹标准化为九类动作的规范形式，设计两个规则模块：Insight识别单轨迹反模式，Converge对比配对轨迹的行为差异。

Result: 函数级选择与完成行为比文件级更能定位成败；反模式主要是整体难度指标，搜索循环最稳定；已解决问题在到达相关代码的速度和无效工作量上仍有差异。

Conclusion: 轨迹结构能为结果添加可审计的诊断上下文，定位审查目标、提出失败假设、优先排查轨迹。

Abstract: Coding agents are ranked almost entirely by resolve rate: whether their final patch passes the target tests. Yet two agents can reach the same outcome through very different processes, and a single pass/fail label says nothing about why a run failed or why an accepted run spent extra steps, time, or tokens. This process evidence lives in the trajectory, which records a run's searches, reads, edits, tool calls, validation, and reversions. However, raw traces are heterogeneous and hard to compare across runs. We present TraceProbe, a trajectory-diagnostic framework that recovers what resolve rate hides. TraceProbe normalizes each raw run into a canonical nine-type action taxonomy with deterministic effect labels, then applies two rule-based modules: Insight names single-trajectory anti-patterns adapted from established debugging practice (e.g., search loops, verification skips), while Converge aligns pairs of runs and classifies where their behavior diverges under controlled references. Applying TraceProbe to 2,500 trajectories from five production settings on SWE-Bench Verified, we find that (i) file choice is too coarse to separate success from failure, whereas function selection and completion behavior localize it; (ii) Insight anti-patterns act mainly as corpus-level difficulty clues, with search loops the most stable; and (iii) even resolved runs differ in how quickly they reach relevant code and how much failed work they incur. Trajectory structure thus adds auditable diagnostic context to outcomes by localizing inspection targets, suggesting failure hypotheses, and prioritizing runs for review.

### [225] [LogicHunter: Testing LLM Agent Frameworks with an Agentic Oracle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06195)
*Minghui Long,Yanjie Zhao,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LogicHunter，一个针对LLM agent框架的模糊测试框架，通过规格驱动生成和智能Agentic Oracle，有效解决了纯Python框架中缺陷难以检测的问题，发现了40个先前未知的bug，其中30个已确认、26个已修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM agent框架（如LangChain、LlamaIndex、CrewAI）在真实AI系统中广泛应用，但严重缺乏有效测试。主要挑战包括：(1) 纯Python框架中缺陷表现为普通异常或静默语义失败，缺乏可靠的测试预言（crash oracle缺失）；(2) Pydantic类型约束和复杂协议导致现有模糊测试器生成大量无效输入；(3) 传统测试生成器只能产生弱回归断言的平凡测试用例。

Method: LogicHunter包含两大核心组件：(1) 规格驱动生成（Specification-driven Generation）——融合形式化类型约束与真实仓库中的典型使用模式，生成语法有效但语义极端的输入，并植入行为探针以暴露静默失败；(2) Agentic Oracle——基于ReAct架构，具备双层状态管理（Dual-Layer State Management）和双流记忆（Dual-Stream Memory），主动检索文档、浏览源码、检查运行时状态，而非被动分类。

Result: 在三个广泛部署的LLM agent框架上评估：(1) 发现40个先前未知bug，其中30个已确认、26个已被开发者修复；(2) 现有的最先进基线方法未能报告任何有效bug；(3) Agentic Oracle达到91.17%的精确率，远超最优被动方法（29.27%），提升61个百分点。

Conclusion: LogicHunter证明了主动规格感知测试在LLM agent框架中的有效性，尤其是在解决预言模糊问题方面，Agentic Oracle的主动推理能力显著优于传统被动分类方法。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agent frameworks such as LangChain, LlamaIndex, and CrewAI have become critical infrastructure powering production AI systems, yet they remain severely under-tested due to fundamental challenges in automated testing. Unlike traditional software, where crashes serve as reliable oracles, defects in these pure Python frameworks manifest as ordinary exceptions or silent semantic failures, creating profound oracle ambiguity. This problem is exacerbated by strict type governance through Pydantic schemas and complex protocol requirements that cause existing fuzzers to generate overwhelming invalid inputs, while traditional test generators produce only trivial cases with weak regression assertions.
  We present LogicHunter, a fuzzing framework that addresses both the generation and oracle challenges through active specification-aware testing. LogicHunter employs specification-driven generation that systematically fuses formal type constraints with authentic usage patterns from real-world repositories, synthesizing inputs that are valid by construction yet semantically extreme, equipped with behavioral probes to expose silent failures. To resolve oracle ambiguity, we introduce the Agentic Oracle, which transcends passive classification by actively retrieving documentation, navigating source code, and inspecting runtime states through a ReAct-based architecture with Dual-Layer State Management and Dual-Stream Memory. Evaluated on three widely deployed frameworks, LogicHunter discovered 40 previously unknown bugs with 30 confirmed and 26 fixed by developers, while state-of-the-art baselines reported no bugs as final findings. The Agentic Oracle achieves 91.17% precision, surpassing the best passive approach at 29.27% by 61 percentage points.

</details>


### [226] [AgentTether: Graph-Guided Diagnosis and Runtime Intervention for Reliable LLM Agent Operation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06273)
*Chenyu Zhao,Shenglin Zhang,Wenwei Gu,Yongqian Sun,Dan Pei,Chetan Bansal,Saravan Rajmohan,Minghua Ma*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AgentTether 是一个无需修改 agent 或环境的运行时修复框架，通过将运行轨迹抽象为转换单元、构建依赖感知的临界转换图，并结合离线正常行为模型与运行时图检测器定位失败子轨迹，进而生成行为范围的修复指导并支持可选的运行时干预，在 tau-bench 的 Banking 任务上分别修复了 59.04% 的 Qwen3.7-max 失败任务和 65.12% 的 GPT-5.4 失败任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM agent 修复方法存在不足：盲目重试无诊断、结果反馈只知失败不知原因、自我反思缺乏证据难以防止失败重复发生。需要一种能自动诊断并引导恢复、且不修改 agent 或环境的运行时修复框架。

Method: 将每次运行抽象为 Transition Units，构建依赖感知的 Critical Transition Graph；结合离线正常行为模型与运行时图检测器定位失败关键子轨迹；将定位到的原因转化为行为范围的修复指导，并由跨迭代的 Repair Memory 支撑；可选地应用带守卫的运行时干预以在重执行期间保持修正。

Result: 在 261 个 tau-bench 任务上评估，Banking 域中 Qwen3.7-max 失败任务修复率 59.04%（49/83），GPT-5.4 失败任务修复率 65.12%（56/86）。整体上提升了修复有效性，同时减少了 agent 轮次和端到端 token 消耗。

Conclusion: AgentTether 可作为实用的可靠性层包裹现有 agent 部署，减少浪费的重执行，提升恢复效果，且无需重新训练 agent。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly used for multi-step, stateful tool-use tasks, yet production reliability remains limited. Unlike static software repair, agent repair must recover dynamic trajectories whose early decisions can propagate into later errors and external state changes. Existing automatic remedies address only part of this problem: blind retry adds no diagnosis, outcome feedback says whether a run failed but not where or why, and self-reflection often lacks grounded evidence to prevent the same failure from recurring. We present AgentTether, a run-time repair framework that automates post-run diagnosis and guided recovery without modifying the underlying agent or environment. AgentTether abstracts each run into Transition Units, links them through a dependency-aware Critical Transition Graph, and localizes failure-critical subtrajectories by combining an offline normal-behavior model with a run-local graph detector. It then converts the localized cause into behavior-scoped guidance backed by cross-iteration Repair Memory, and can optionally apply guarded run-time intervention to keep the correction active during re-execution. The same design can be deployed as an offline diagnostic-and-guidance tool or as an online repair layer.
  We evaluate AgentTether on 261 tau-bench tasks across three domains with Qwen3.7-max, and test cross-model transfer on Banking with GPT-5.4. On the hardest Banking domain, AgentTether repairs 59.04% (49/83) of initially failed Qwen3.7-max tasks and 65.12% (56/86) of initially failed GPT-5.4 tasks. Overall, AgentTether improves repair effectiveness while reducing agent turns and end-to-end approach tokens, suggesting a practical reliability layer that can wrap existing agent deployments, reduce wasted re-execution, and improve recovery without retraining the agent.

</details>


### [227] [UI2App: Benchmarking Visual Interaction Inference in Executable Web Application Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06306)
*Grace Man Chen,Litao Guo,Yifan Wu,Yiyu Chen,Yenchi Tseng,Sicheng Liu,Yuyu Luo,Ying-Cong Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: UI2App是首个针对交互推理能力的基准测试，包含327张截图和45组状态连贯的截图集，用于评估模型从静态截图恢复多路由Web应用交互行为的能力。实验发现六个前沿视觉语言模型在视觉重建和交互实现之间存在显著能力鸿沟，最高交互得分仅7.5，跨页面状态等高复杂度交互仍是瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估视觉保真度，缺乏对生成工件交互能力的系统评估。为填补这一空白，提出UI2App基准，专门测试模型从静态截图推断应用交互行为的能力。

Method: 构建包含327张截图、45组状态连贯截图集的基准，设计端到端流水线从四个维度（可执行性、导航可达性、视觉保真度、交互推理）评估生成工件。交互度量(IIS)按功能正确性和状态管理复杂度评估推断交互，不依赖单一参考。

Result: 六个前沿视觉语言模型在视觉重建和交互实现间存在显著能力鸿沟。视觉保真度领先的模型在IIS上仅得7.5分，排名第四，落后IIS领先者5.2倍。半数模型在跨页面状态等高复杂度交互维度上得分为零。

Conclusion: 从静态截图推断完整交互行为仍是当前模型面临的关键挑战，现有模型在交互推理能力上存在严重不足。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated growing competence in web page generation. However, existing text-driven approaches rely on complex prompts that impose substantial demands on users and offer limited expressivity for page layout and cross-page visual coherence. Image-driven paradigms, which take UI screenshots as input, align more closely with real development workflows. However, current benchmarks focus primarily on visual fidelity and lack a systematic evaluation of the interaction capabilities in generated artifacts. To address this gap, we introduce UI2App, the first benchmark targeting interaction inference, the ability to recover application behavior from screenshots alone, without any textual or behavioral guidance. UI2App comprises 327 screenshots grouped into 45 state-coherent screenshot sets for runnable multi-route web applications. We design an end-to-end pipeline that evaluates each artifact along four dimensions: executability, navigation reachability, visual fidelity, and interaction inference. The interaction metric (IIS) assesses inferred interactions by functional correctness and state-management complexity, crediting any valid implementation rather than matching a single reference. Experiments on six frontier vision-language models reveal a marked capability mismatch between visual reconstruction and interaction realization: the visual-fidelity leader scores only 7.5 on IIS, ranking fourth and trailing the IIS leader by 5.2x. High-complexity interactions such as cross-page state remain a pervasive bottleneck, with half of the evaluated models scoring exactly zero on this dimension. Overall, the results indicate that inferring complete interaction behavior from static screenshots remains a key challenge for models.

</details>


### [228] [RuBench: A Repository-Level Agentic Coding Benchmark with Natively Authored Russian Task Specifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06411)
*Evgeny Shilov*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: RuBench 1.0 是一个包含25个俄罗斯语自然语言描述的仓库级代码修复基准测试，评估5款主流编码代理产品在真实维护场景下的表现。最佳配置解决78.7%的任务，同时发现产品会静默替换模型（20%的任务中），证明真正被评估的是产品而非模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仓库级代理基准测试的任务描述均为英文，但实际开发中越来越多开发者用母语（如俄语）以客户请求风格描述任务，现有基准无法衡量这种真实场景。作者希望填补这一空白。

Method: 从5个开源仓库（aiohttp、aiogram、Laravel、NestJS、Fastify）的近期修复提交中挖掘25个任务，每个任务用俄语从零编写（模拟真实客户请求，非翻译）。用上游维护者的回归测试作为评判标准，且测试集不公开。评估多个生产级配置（Claude Code + 不同模型、Codex CLI + GPT-5.5），每配置运行3次，报告pass@1、置信区间、成本等。

Result: 最佳配置（Claude Code + Sonnet 5等）解决78.7%的任务。由于N=25，仅最弱模型与最强之间的差距在统计上显著。审计发现一个配置中20%的任务（5/25）被产品安全机制静默回退到Opus 4.8，证明评估的是产品整体而非模型本身。

Conclusion: RuBench 1.0 填补了多语言、真实风格任务描述的基准空白。核心结论：部署的编码代理产品（而非底层模型）才是真正应被评估的单位，因为产品层可能引入模型替换等不可见行为。发布任务描述、轨迹等内容，但评分测试集保持不公开。

Abstract: Developers increasingly delegate real maintenance work to product-grade coding agents, and many state tasks in their native language, in the style of a customer request rather than a curated English issue. Existing repository-level agentic benchmarks do not measure this setting: their task statements are English by design. We introduce RuBench 1.0, a benchmark of 25 tasks mined from recent fix commits in five live open-source repositories (aiohttp, aiogram, Laravel, NestJS, Fastify; Python, PHP, TypeScript, JavaScript), where each task is specified natively in Russian -- written from scratch in the style of an actual customer request, not translated -- and judged by the upstream maintainer's regression tests, which we withhold from release. All 25 fix commits postdate the training-data cutoffs of every evaluated model, giving a contamination argument that holds task-by-task. We evaluate deployed product configurations (CLI agent + model + reasoning effort) -- Claude Code with Opus 4.8, Sonnet 5, and Haiku 4.5, and Codex CLI with GPT-5.5 -- with three independent runs each, reporting pass@1 with task-level confidence intervals, paired comparisons, dollar cost, and token usage. The best configuration resolves 78.7% of tasks; at N=25 only the gaps to the weakest model are statistically resolvable, which we state explicitly. Auditing full trajectories of a fifth, hors-concours configuration (Claude Code + Fable 5, July 2, 2026 release), we caught the product silently substituting the model: on 5 of 25 tasks (20%) an official safeguard fallback re-routed routine HTTP-protocol fixes to Opus 4.8 -- direct, reproducible evidence that the deployed product, not the model, is the unit actually measured. We release task statements, metadata, full agent trajectories, and diffs; grading oracles are withheld, with a SHA-256 manifest committed at publication time.

### [229] [Domain-Driven Design in Practice: A Large-Scale Empirical Characterisation of the Open-Source Ecosystem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06471)
*Ozan Özkan,Önder Babur,Mark van den Brand*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究通过挖掘GitHub上11,742个候选仓库（经GPT-4o三重验证后保留2,502个），首次大规模刻画了领域驱动设计（DDD）的实践图景。研究发现DDD采用在2017年后加速，项目寿命远超典型GitHub项目，C#和TypeScript实际领先Java，但25.3%的项目缺乏明确的业务上下文记录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DDD研究多为理论性，缺乏大规模实证评估。前期工作发现近39%的DDD研究缺少严格的实证评价，因此需要基于真实数据建立DDD实践现状的基线。

Method: 采用软件仓库挖掘（MSR）方法：首先通过主题模型和README关键词混合策略识别11,742个候选仓库；然后构建基于GPT-4o的三重多数投票语义验证流水线，最终获得2,502个已验证仓库；并通过人工标注样本验证（kappa=0.77）。

Result: DDD采用在2017年后显著加速；项目中位寿命远超典型GitHub项目一个数量级；分层架构和整洁架构占主导；CQRS和事件溯源常见于分布式数据密集型系统；C#和TypeScript领先Java；25.3%的项目无明确业务上下文记录。

Conclusion: DDD已成熟为稳定的专业级实践，跨语言和领域被广泛采用。但四分之一项目缺乏业务上下文记录，暴露了领域意图设计与版本控制保存之间的持续差距。呼吁建立轻量级架构可追溯性标准，并为复用这些仓库提供指导。

Abstract: Context: Domain-Driven Design (DDD) is a leading paradigm for managing software complexity, yet research remains largely theoretical; our prior work found nearly 39% of DDD studies lack rigorous empirical evaluation, leaving practical adoption largely unexamined at scale. Objective: We provide the first large-scale characterisation of the DDD landscape on GitHub, a data-driven baseline for how the paradigm is implemented and sustained in practice. Method: Using a Mining Software Repositories (MSR) approach with a hybrid strategy (topics and README keywords), we identified 11,742 candidate repositories. To address label noise, we built a novel semantic validation pipeline using GPT-4o with a triplicate majority-vote strategy, yielding 2,502 verified repositories. Validation against a manually labelled sample showed substantial agreement with human experts (kappa = 0.77). Results: DDD adoption accelerated sharply after a 2017 inflection point, and the resulting projects are notably long-lived: their median lifespan exceeds the typical GitHub project by over an order of magnitude, indicating sustained, professional-grade engineering rather than short-lived experiments. Layered and Clean Architecture dominate, while CQRS and Event Sourcing recur in distributed, data-intensive systems. Notably, the data challenge the Java-centric assumption of much academic work: C# and TypeScript, not Java, lead practical adoption. Conclusions: DDD has matured into a stable, professional-grade practice adopted across diverse languages and domains. However, a quarter of projects (25.3%) record no explicit business context, revealing a persistent gap between how domain intent is designed and how it is preserved in version control. We call for lightweight architectural traceability standards and offer guidance for teams reusing these repositories as reference implementations.

### [230] [Industry Classification of GitHub Repositories Using the North American Industry Classification System (NAICS)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06505)
*Kevin Xu,Alexander Quispe*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了NAICS-GH，一个包含6,588个GitHub仓库并被标注了NAICS行业分类的公开数据集，通过检索-验证管道实现96.98%的精度，并开源了数据集、代码和模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GitHub上有数亿公开仓库，但缺乏从仓库到标准化行业分类的原生映射，阻碍了创新地理学、开源生产的产业构成以及新技术跨行业扩散的实证研究。

Method: 采用检索-验证管道：先用BAAI/bge-large-en嵌入和FAISS检索从约137万源仓库中筛选出31,178个候选仓库-行业对，再用GPT-4.1基于评分标准进行验证，保留得分≥8的6,588个高置信度标签。

Result: 管道再现性达0.03%误差以内；在2,421个人工验证随机样本上标签精度为96.98%（Wilson 95%置信区间[96.23, 97.59]）；RoBERTa-large在20%测试集上F1达86.45%，准确率86.35%。

Conclusion: 该数据集和管道可有效填补GitHub仓库到行业分类的映射空白，所有资源以CC-BY-4.0和MIT许可证开源发布。

Abstract: GitHub hosts hundreds of millions of public repositories, but the platform exposes no native mapping from repositories to standardized industry sectors. This gap limits empirical work on the geography of innovation, the industrial composition of open-source production, and the diffusion of new technologies across economic sectors. We present NAICS-GH, a publicly released corpus of 6,588 GitHub repositories drawn from source pools covering the United States, the European Union, and Australia, each labeled with a 2-digit sector from the North American Industry Classification System (NAICS 2022). Labels are produced by a retrieve-and-verify pipeline that combines BAAI/bge-large-en embeddings, FAISS retrieval, and GPT-4.1 rubric scoring. The pipeline narrows about 1.37 million source repositories to 31,178 candidate repository-sector pairs and retains 6,588 high-confidence labels with score at least 8. Re-running the retrieval pipeline end to end reproduces the candidate set to within 0.03 percent. On a 2,421-repository human-validated random sample, the released labels attain 96.98 percent precision, with Wilson 95 percent confidence interval [96.23, 97.59]. We benchmark six pretrained encoders on the released corpus; RoBERTa-large reaches 86.45 percent F1 and 86.35 percent accuracy on a held-out 20 percent test set. The dataset, Croissant metadata, pipeline code, prompts, and fine-tuned checkpoint are released under CC-BY-4.0 and MIT licenses.

### [231] [Fusion or Confusion? Potential and Challenges in Fusion of Onboard Sensors and V2X Data in Cooperative Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05889)
*Amir Mohammadisarab,Miguel Sepulcre,Luca Lusvarghi,Sergei S. Avedisov,Mohammad Irfan Khan,Takayuki Shimizu,Onur Altintas,Javier Gozalvez*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了网联自动驾驶汽车（CAV）中，车载传感器与V2X协同感知数据的融合问题，发现V2X渗透率提升虽可改善感知能力，但数据噪声会导致大量假阳性（幽灵目标），即使高精度V2X数据也可能产生虚假目标，威胁安全与效率，强调了鲁棒融合方法的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对协同感知已有关注，但鲜有深入分析V2X数据（通过协同感知消息传输）与车载传感器信息融合过程中，数据数量与质量对融合结果的影响，尤其是假阳性幽灵目标的产生机制。

Method: 通过实验探究车载传感器与V2X数据融合过程，分析V2X渗透率、数据准确性对感知效果的影响，并观察假阳性幽灵目标的出现条件。

Result: ①V2X渗透率提升可显著降低环境感知不确定性；②但若V2X数据不够准确，会引入大量假阳性；③即使V2X数据准确，幽灵目标仍可能出现，威胁安全与驾驶效率。

Conclusion: 协同感知面临假阳性挑战，需发展鲁棒的数据融合方法；该发现对ETSI TS 103 324等标准化工作具有重要意义。

Abstract: Connected Automated Vehicles (CAVs) utilize their onboard sensors to perceive the environment. The perception range and accuracy can be affected by adverse weather or non-line-of-sight conditions. Cooperative perception or sensor sharing can overcome these limitations by enabling CAVs to exchange sensor data, thus collectively enhancing their perception capabilities. Previous studies have shown the potential of cooperative perception, but limited attention has been given to the fusion of V2X data received through cooperative perception messages with onboard sensor information. The fusion process can be influenced by the quantity and quality of the V2X data. An increased volume of V2X data can reduce uncertainty in the perceived environment; however, when the data is noisy, it may compromise the accuracy of the fusion results. This study investigates the fusion of onboard sensor and V2X data in cooperative perception, and demonstrates that while perception can significantly improve as the V2X penetration rate increases, it can introduce a significant number of false positives if V2X data is not highly accurate. False positives result in the detection of ghost objects that do not actually exist. These ghost objects can, in turn, compromise safety and driving efficiency. Our analysis found that false positives or ghost objects can appear even with accurate V2X data. These findings highlight the challenges in cooperative perception and the importance of developing robust data fusion methods to enhance the reliability of cooperative perception. This is particularly relevant in light of ongoing standardization efforts, such as ETSI TS 103 324 on collective perception.

### [232] [Agentic AI for IPoDWDM Network Lifecycle Automation: An MCP-Enabled Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05958)
*Chunmin Xia,Jakub Harbaczewski,Nikhil Dsilva,Julie Raulin,Dominic Schneider,Achim Autenrieth*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出了一种分布式、厂商无关的多MCP架构，用于多厂商多层的IPoDWDM网络的自动化与自治控制，实现了端到端服务生命周期自动化和跨层闭环控制，并在实验平台上验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多厂商、多层的IPoDWDM网络在自动化和自治控制方面存在挑战，缺乏统一的、厂商无关的架构来实现端到端的服务生命周期管理和跨层闭环控制。

Method: 提出一种分布式多MCP（Multi-MCP）架构，通过SDN实现厂商无关的自动化控制，利用GNPy模型和光层遥测技术实现跨层闭环控制。

Result: 在IPoDWDM实验平台上成功验证了该架构的有效性，实现了端到端服务生命周期自动化和闭环跨层控制。

Conclusion: 该分布式多MCP架构能够有效实现多厂商多层级IPoDWDM网络的自动化与自治控制，具有厂商无关性和可扩展性。

Abstract: We present a distributed, vendor-agnostic multi-MCP architecture for SDN-based automation and autonomous control of multi-vendor, multi-layer IPoDWDM networks. The framework enables E2E service lifecycle automation, closed-loop cross-layer control using GNPy model and optical telemetry, and is experimentally validated on a IPoDWDM testbed.

</details>

*Chunmin Xia,Jakub Harbaczewski,Nikhil Dsilva,Julie Raulin,Dominic Schneider,Achim Autenrieth*

Abstract: This demo presents an MCP-enabled agentic AI architecture for autonomous control of vendor-agnostic IPoDWDM networks. We demonstrate live end-to-end lifecycle multi-layer automation and closed-loop control using GNPy and telemetry, validated on a real testbed.

### [234] [FLAIR: Distributed Federated Learning with Dynamic Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06025)
*Ihssan Boutebicha,Bilel Zaghdoudi,Mohamed Amine Legheraba,Maria Potop Butucaru*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: FLAIR 是一种完全去中心化的联邦学习协议，通过动态、资源感知的安全自组织聚类和可验证的簇头选举机制，在传感器网络等无基础设施环境中实现了高可扩展性、鲁棒性和性能，在100节点静态网络中达到约0.91的准确率，即使在90%节点故障下仍保持0.85以上准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的集中式和分层联邦学习架构在动态、无基础设施的环境（如传感器网络）中存在可扩展性差、鲁棒性不足以及单点故障等问题，亟需一种完全去中心化的解决方案。

Method: 提出了 FLAIR 协议，核心包括：(1) 动态、资源感知的安全自组织聚类；(2) 簇内模型训练；(3) 基于概率的可验证簇头选举机制，该机制优先选择计算和通信能力更强的节点，兼顾公平与效率。

Result: 在ns-3仿真中，FLAIR在静态100节点网络中准确率约0.91，优于所有基线；在90%节点故障下准确率仍高于0.85；移动部署下性能损失小于2%；在智能农业仿真中准确率与集中式基线仅差0.2%。

Conclusion: FLAIR成功将去中心化学习的可扩展性与聚类的结构效率相结合，为大规模异构物联网系统提供了一种鲁棒且高性能的解决方案。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) offers a privacy-preserving framework for distributed machine learning, yet conventional centralized and hierarchical architectures present significant challenges in terms of scalability, resilience, and single points of failure, particularly in dynamic, infrastructure-less environments such as sensor networks. To address these limitations, we introduce FLAIR, a novel, fully decentralized FL protocol that integrates dynamic, resource-aware secure and self-organized clustering with in-cluster model training. FLAIR leverages a probabilistic, verifiable cluster-head election mechanism, which is enhanced to favor nodes with greater computational and communication capabilities, thereby ensuring both fairness and efficiency. Through comprehensive simulations in ns-3, we evaluate FLAIR against centralized, hierarchical, and gossip-based FL benchmarks across four demanding scenarios. The results demonstrate the superiority of our approach: in static 100-node networks, FLAIR achieves a final accuracy of approximately 0.91, outperforming all baselines. The protocol exhibits exceptional robustness, maintaining graceful degradation with accuracy above 0.85 even under 90% node failure rates. Furthermore, it shows strong resilience to mobility, with a performance loss of less than 2% compared to static deployments. In a realistic smart farming simulation, FLAIR's accuracy is within 0.2% of the centralized baseline, confirming its practical viability. These findings validate that FLAIR successfully combines the scalability of decentralized learning with the structural efficiency of clustering, presenting a robust and high performing solution for large-scale, heterogeneous IoT systems.

</details>


### [235] [Packet Routing for the Quantum Internet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06075)
*Robert Malaney*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出在现有IPv6协议基础上，通过利用扩展头（Extension Headers）功能，以最小改动实现量子数据包路由，支持量子隐形传态、量子路由及这些过程的叠加态操作，为量子互联网提供一种新的路由架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子互联网路由方案改动较大，作者希望以最小化修改现有标准（IPv6）的方式，利用IPv6中未被充分利用的扩展头功能，实现量子路由能力，从而降低部署门槛。

Method: 基于IPv6扩展头机制进行最小化改动，设计支持量子隐形传态、量子路由及其叠加态操作的量子数据包路由架构，不追求最优性，而是探索通过小改动激发新的量子路由可能性。

Result: 相较于其他量子互联网路由方案，该架构能够实现更广泛的量子力学允许的结果，增加了量子路由的灵活性和可能性。

Conclusion: 该设计提供了一条通过小幅扩充现有IPv6协议来开启量子路由新可能性的路径，虽未声称最优，但为量子互联网的实际部署提供了务实思路。

Abstract: We present a new design for quantum packet routing within the emerging Quantum Internet, highlighting how a little-used feature of Internet Protocol Version 6 (IPv6), namely Extension Headers, can lead to a significant amount of quantumness within the IP layer. Taking a minimalist approach to alterations of established standards, we outline the changes required in order for quantum teleportation, quantum routing, and superpositions of these processes to be enabled. Relative to other proposals for routing within the Quantum Internet, the architecture we propose enables a wider range of outcomes allowed by quantum mechanics. We do not claim any optimally in our design, but rather a pathway to invoke new quantum routing outcomes via small additions to the current IPv6.

</details>


### [236] [Repeated Contention Scheduling: A Novel Resource Allocation Algorithm Toward 6G Vehicular Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06103)
*Alexey Rolich,Marco Tricco,Simone Paroli,Mert Yildiz,Andrea Baiocchi*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 针对NR-V2X侧行链路中资源分配效率低下的问题，提出了一种基于多轮反馈竞争的重复竞争调度（RCS）算法，通过消除长期预留实现全分布式操作，在成功概率、碰撞损失降低和信息时效性方面显著优于传统SPS和DS方案，并通过SDR实验平台验证了实际可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半持续调度（SPS）和动态调度（DS）在动态密集场景下存在持续碰撞和适应性不足的问题，亟需一种更高效的去中心化资源分配方案。

Method: 提出重复竞争调度（RCS），一种基于多轮反馈驱动竞争的分布式资源分配算法，不依赖长期预留，实现完全分布式操作。

Result: 仿真结果表明RCS在成功概率、碰撞与丢包率、信息时效性（如包间接收时延和信息年龄）等指标上均优于SPS和DS，尤其在高负载场景下优势显著。SDR实验验证了在实际硬件条件下算法的鲁棒性，结果与理论分析及仿真高度吻合。

Conclusion: RCS是一种可行且可扩展的5G NR侧行链路资源分配方案，也是未来6G车联网通信系统的有力候选技术。

Abstract: Efficient decentralized resource allocation remains a fundamental challenge in NR-V2X sidelink communications, where conventional Semi-Persistent Scheduling (SPS) and Dynamic Scheduling (DS) suffer from persistent collisions and limited adaptability under dynamic and dense conditions. This paper proposes Repeated Contention Scheduling (RCS), a novel resource allocation algorithm based on multi-round, feedback-driven contention that eliminates long-term reservations and enables fully distributed operation. Simulations demonstrate that RCS outperforms SPS and DS in terms of success probability, collision and loss reduction, and timeliness metrics such as Packet Inter-Reception Delay and Age of Information, particularly under high load. The practical feasibility of the approach is validated through an SDR-based experimental testbed, which confirms robust operation under realistic hardware impairments and closely matches theoretical and simulation results. These findings establish RCS as a viable and scalable solution for resource allocation in 5G NR sidelink and a promising candidate for future 6G vehicular communication systems.

</details>


### [237] [Quality-Aware Personalized AI Service Provisioning in UAV-Assisted 6G Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06278)
*Mohammad Farhoudi,Masoud Shokrnezhad,Tarik Taleb*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出HyPE框架，结合移动性预测、LLM推理增强决策与启发式服务部署，在无人机辅助的6G网络中实现兼顾传统服务质量与AI服务质量（输出保真度、连续性、个性化）的弹性AI服务供应，仿真结果优于优化方法和现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有6G AI服务方法仅关注传统服务质量（如延迟），忽视了AI服务质量维度（输出保真度、连续性、个性化），尤其在动态空地场景中无法实现个性化服务供应。

Method: HyPE框架包含三部分：(i) 移动性感知预测，预报时空请求分布；(ii) 基于大语言模型推理的学习增强决策，优化无人机轨迹与推理任务分配；(iii) 预处理/后处理的服务放置与路由启发式算法。整体作为联合轨迹规划、服务放置与路由优化问题的高可扩展近似方案。

Result: 在实证移动轨迹与异构AI工作负载仿真下，HyPE相比优化方法和现有基线，实现了近最优覆盖率、更低的端到端延迟，并持续保持了AI服务质量驱动的个性化服务。

Conclusion: 预测性学习增强服务供应是实现6G中弹性、以用户为中心的AI服务的有前景方案。

Abstract: In sixth-generation (6G) artificial intelligence (AI) services, two quality dimensions should be jointly addressed: conventional quality (e.g., latency) and Quality of AI Services (QoAIS; output fidelity, continuity, personalization). Existing methods emphasize conventional quality, while neglecting QoAIS, particularly for personalized outputs in dynamic aerial-terrestrial settings. This paper introduces HyPE, a Hybrid Predictive-in-context-lEarning framework for holistically quality-aware personalized AI service provisioning in Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV)-assisted 6G networks. HyPE integrates: (i) mobility-aware prediction to forecast spatio-temporal request distributions, (ii) learning-augmented decision leveraging Large Language Model (LLM)-based reasoning to optimize UAV trajectories and inference assignments, and (iii) pre-/post-processing service placement and routing using heuristics. We formulate an optimization problem for joint trajectory planning, service placement, and routing, and present HyPE as a scalable alternative to intractable optimal solutions. Simulations with empirical mobility traces and heterogeneous AI workloads show near-optimal coverage, reduced end-to-end latency, sustained QoAIS-driven, and continuity-based service personalization versus optimization and state-of-the-art baselines. The results highlight the promise of predictive learning-augmented provisioning for elastic, user-centric AI in 6G.

</details>

### [238] [TMF-RSE: Tri-Modal Fusion with Regional Semantics and Evidential Uncertainty for Lung Severity Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06356)
*Fadi Abdeladhim Zidi,Salah Eddine Bekhouche,Abdellah Zakaria Sellam,Gaby Maroun,Fadi Dornaika,Cosimo Distante*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 提出TMF-RSE三模态深度学习框架，融合2D影像外观、肺分割结构特征和视觉-语言模型语义特征，通过互补融合机制和证据回归，实现肺部疾病严重程度量化，在Per-COVID-19 CT和RALO数据集上优于最新Transformer基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从胸部影像中准确量化肺部疾病严重程度对临床决策和资源分配至关重要，现有方法在充分利用多模态信息方面存在不足。

Method: 提出TMF-RSE三模态融合框架：1)融合2D胸部影像的外观特征、肺部分割掩膜的结构特征、视觉-语言模型(VLM)的语义特征；2)采用互补融合机制实现语义引导、结构先验和层级跨模态交互；3)使用证据回归同时提供严重程度预测和不确定性估计。

Result: 在Per-COVID-19 CT上MAE为4.02，Pearson相关系数0.9629；在RALO地理范围评估上MAE为0.339，PC为0.973，均优于最近Transformer基线方法。

Conclusion: TMF-RSE通过三模态融合有效提升了肺部疾病严重程度量化的准确性，并提供了不确定性估计，具有临床应用潜力。

Abstract: Accurate quantification of lung disease severity from chest imaging is critical for clinical decision-making and resource allocation. We propose a tri-modal deep learning framework, TMF-RSE (Tri-Modal Fusion with Regional Semantics and Evidential Uncertainty), that combines appearance features from two-dimensional chest inputs, structural features from lung segmentation masks, and semantic features from vision-language models (VLMs) for severity quantification. Our approach employs complementary fusion mechanisms that integrate semantic guidance, structural priors, and hierarchical interactions across modalities. The model employs evidential regression to provide both severity predictions and uncertainty estimates. Experiments on the Per-COVID-19 CT and RALO datasets show that TMF-RSE outperforms recent transformer-based baselines, achieving MAE of 4.02 and Pearson correlation of 0.9629 on Per-COVID-19 validation, and 0.339 MAE / 0.973 PC on RALO geographic extent.

</details>
